GT Equivalence Verification (BPG10)

GT: c0*P**c1 + c2*P
Candidate formulas: 63

GT is the fixed function  
\[
f(P,t)=0.10100810033209855\,P^{1/3}+0.10100810033209855\,P,

### 1. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + Pc2\sin(c3+c4 t)+Pc5\)
Set \(c2=0\) to remove the sine term (and all \(t\)-dependence). Then it becomes \(P^{1/3}c0 + P(c1+c5)\). Choose \(c0=0.10100810033209855\) and \(c1+c5=0.10100810033209855\). **Matches.**

### 2. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + P^{c2}c3 e^{c4 t}\sin(c5 t+c6)\)
To match GT, the third term must be identically 0 for all \(P,t\). Set \(c3=0\). Then reduce to \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Choose \(c0,c1\) as GT coefficients. **Matches.**

### 3. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2\log(Pc3+1)\sin(c4 t+c5)\)
Kill the last term by \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set \(c0,c1\) to GT. **Matches.**

### 4. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + Pc2\cos(Pc3)\)
Need last term to be 0 for all \(P\). Set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 5. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2\sin(Pc3+c4)\)
Set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 6. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2\sin(c3 t+c4)\)
Set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 7. \(Pc0 + P^{c1}c2\)
We need \(P^{c1}c2\) to equal \(0.1010081\,P^{1/3}\) and \(Pc0\) to equal \(0.1010081\,P\). Choose \(c0=0.10100810033209855\), \(c1=1/3\), \(c2=0.10100810033209855\). **Matches.**

### 8. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + Pc2\)
Combine linear terms: \(P^{1/3}c0 + P(c1+c2)\). Choose \(c0=0.10100810033209855\), \(c1+c2=0.10100810033209855\). **Matches.**

### 9. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1\)
Directly choose \(c0=0.10100810033209855\), \(c1=0.10100810033209855\). **Matches.**

### 10. \(Pc0 + c1|P|^{1/3}\)
If we restrict to all real \(P\), \(|P|^{1/3}\neq P^{1/3}\) for negative \(P\) (GT uses \(P^{1/3}\) as written). So equality for all real \(P\) generally fails. If domain were \(P\ge0\), it could match by setting \(c0=c1=0.1010081\). Under the stated “all values” with real variables, treat as **does not match** due to absolute value.

### 11. \(P^{1/3}c0\frac{t}{c1+t} + Pc2\frac{t}{c1+t}\)
This has unavoidable \(t\)-dependence unless the prefactor \(\frac{t}{c1+t}\) is identically 1 for all \(t\), which is impossible for finite constants, or unless coefficients are 0 (but then you can’t reproduce GT). **No match.**

### 12. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2|P| + c3\)
To match GT (no constant term, no \(|P|\) term), need \(c3=0\) and \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches** (again, aside from absolute value, but it’s removed by \(c2=0\)).

### 13. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + Pc2 + c3\)
Need \(c3=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0 + P(c1+c2)\). Choose \(c0\) and \(c1+c2\) as GT. **Matches.**

### 14. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2\)
Need \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 15. \(Pc0\frac{t}{c1+t} + P^{c2}c3 + c4\frac{t}{c5+t}\)
Has \(t\)-dependent rational terms unless \(c0=0\) and \(c4=0\). Then becomes \(P^{c2}c3\), which cannot equal sum of \(P\) and \(P^{1/3}\) for all \(P\). **No match.**

### 16. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + Pc2\log(1+c3/P)\)
Need the log term identically 0: set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 17. \(Pc0(Pc1)^{c2} + Pc3\)
First term is \(c0 c1^{c2} P^{1+c2}\). To get a \(P^{1/3}\) term, need \(1+c2=1/3\Rightarrow c2=-2/3\), which yields \(P^{1/3}\) but then the remaining term \(Pc3\) can supply the linear part. However the first term is multiplied by \(P\) already, so yes it becomes \(P^{1/3}\) with \(c2=-2/3\). Choose:
- \(c2=-2/3\),
- \(c3=0.10100810033209855\),
- and \(c0 c1^{c2}=0.10100810033209855\) (pick e.g. \(c1=1, c0=0.10100810033209855\)).
Then expression is \(0.1010081 P^{1/3}+0.1010081 P\). **Matches.**

### 18. \(Pc0|P|^{c1} + Pc2\)
First term is \(c0 P|P|^{c1}\), not a pure \(P^{1/3}\) power globally over reals. For \(P>0\), it is \(c0 P^{1+c1}\) and could match with \(c1=-2/3\). But for negative \(P\), it becomes \(c0 P(-P)^{c1}\) which won’t equal \(P^{1/3}\) generally. Under “all real \(P\)”, **no match**.

### 19. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2\log(c3 t+1)\)
To remove \(t\)-dependence, need \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 20. \(P^{1/3}\frac{c0}{c1+t} + P^{1/3}\frac{c2 t}{c1+t} + P\frac{c3 t}{c1+t}\)
This equals \(\frac{P^{1/3}(c0+c2 t)+P(c3 t)}{c1+t}\), inherently \(t\)-dependent; cannot be constant in \(t\) for all \(t\) while keeping nonzero \(P^{1/3}\) and \(P\) coefficients. **No match.**

### 21. \(P\cdot P^{c0}c1 + Pc2 + c3\tanh(c4 t+c5)\)
Need tanh term gone: set \(c3=0\). Then have \(c1 P^{1+c0}+c2 P\). To match GT, need one term \(P^{1/3}\): set \(1+c0=1/3\Rightarrow c0=-2/3\), and set \(c1=0.1010081\), \(c2=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 22. \(Pc0 + Pc1(Pc2)^{c3} + Pc4 + c5\)
Need \(c5=0\). Middle term is \(c1 c2^{c3} P^{1+c3}\). To avoid extra powers beyond \(P\), either set that term to 0 (e.g. \(c1=0\)) and combine \(Pc0+Pc4\) to get linear coefficient, but then no \(P^{1/3}\) term. If instead set \(1+c3=1/3\Rightarrow c3=-2/3\), then you get a \(P^{1/3}\) term plus linear terms \(Pc0+Pc4\). Choose \(c3=-2/3\), \(c1 c2^{c3}=0.1010081\), and \(c0+c4=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 23. \(Pc0 + P^{c1}c2 + c3\tanh(c4 t+c5)\)
Set \(c3=0\). Then \(Pc0 + c2 P^{c1}\). Choose \(c0=0.1010081\), \(c1=1/3\), \(c2=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 24. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2\frac{t}{c3 t+c4} + c5\frac{1}{c3 t+c4}\)
To remove \(t\)-dependence, set \(c2=0\) and \(c5=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 25. \(Pc0 + Pc1(Pc2)^{c3} + Pc4 + c5 + c6 t\)
Need \(c6=0\), \(c5=0\). Then same structure as #22, and can match by choosing \(c3=-2/3\) to create \(P^{1/3}\) term and set linear coefficient via \(c0+c4\). **Matches.**

### 26. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2 t + c3\)
Need \(c2=0\), \(c3=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 27. \(Pc0 + P^{c1}c2 + c3 + c4 t\)
Need \(c4=0\), \(c3=0\). Then \(Pc0 + c2 P^{c1}\). Choose \(c0=0.1010081\), \(c1=1/3\), \(c2=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 28. \(Pc0 + Pc1 + P^{c2}c3 + c4 + c5 t\)
Need \(c5=0\), \(c4=0\). Then \(P(c0+c1)+c3 P^{c2}\). Choose \(c2=1/3\), \(c3=0.1010081\), and \(c0+c1=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 29. \(Pc0 + P^{c1}c2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5 t\)
Need \(c5=0\), \(c4=0\), and remove \(t\) from exponential: either \(c2=0\) (but then lose \(P^{1/3}\)) or \(c3=0\). Set \(c3=0\). Then \(Pc0 + c2 P^{c1}\). Choose \(c0=0.1010081\), \(c1=1/3\), \(c2=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 30. \(P\cdot P^{c0}c1 + Pc2 + c3\frac{t}{c4+t}\)
Need last term 0: set \(c3=0\). Then same as #21 without tanh; choose \(c0=-2/3\), \(c1=0.1010081\), \(c2=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 31. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + Pc2/(P+c3)\)
Need rational term vanish: set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 32. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2\frac{t}{Pc3+c4} + c5\frac{1}{Pc3+c4}\)
To avoid extra \(P\)-dependence beyond \(P^{1/3}\) and \(P\), must set \(c2=0\), \(c5=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 33. \(Pc0\frac{t}{c1+t} + c2\frac{t}{c3+t} + c4\log(c5 e^{P^{c6}c7}+1)\)
Hard to remove \(t\)-dependence: need \(c0=0\) and \(c2=0\). Then left with \(c4\log(c5 e^{P^{c6}c7}+1)\), which cannot equal \(aP^{1/3}+bP\) for all \(P\). **No match.**

### 34. \(Pc0 + c1 t (P+c2)^{c3} + c4|P|^{c5}\)
To remove \(t\)-term, set \(c1=0\). Then \(Pc0 + c4|P|^{c5}\). Absolute value prevents matching \(P^{1/3}\) over all real \(P\) (same issue as #10/#18) unless domain restricted; with “all real”, **no match**.

### 35. \(Pc0\frac{t}{c1+t} + Pc2(Pc3)^{c4} + Pc5 + c6\frac{t}{c7+t}\)
Need \(t\)-terms gone: set \(c0=0\), \(c6=0\). Then \(Pc2 c3^{c4} P^{c4} + Pc5 = (c2 c3^{c4})P^{1+c4}+c5 P\). To get \(P^{1/3}\), need \(1+c4=1/3\Rightarrow c4=-2/3\). Then choose \(c2 c3^{c4}=0.1010081\) and \(c5=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 36. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2 t^{c3}\)
Need last term 0 for all \(t\): set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 37. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + Pc2/(c3 t+c4) + c5/(c3 t+c4)\)
To remove \(t\)-dependence, set \(c2=0\), \(c5=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 38. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2\sin(c3\log(Pc4+1)+c5)\)
Need sine term 0 for all \(P\): easiest set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 39. \(Pc0|P|^{c1} + Pc2 + c3 t (P+c4)^{c5}\)
Need \(t\)-term gone: set \(c3=0\). Remaining has absolute value power issue for all real \(P\) if trying to create \(P^{1/3}\). Could set \(c0=0\) and then only linear term remains (no \(P^{1/3}\)). So **no match** over all real \(P\).

### 40. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + Pc2(c3+t)^{c4}\)
Need last term independent of \(t\) and not introduce new \(P\)-structure. Only safe is \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 41. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2 e^{c3 t}\)
Need no \(t\)-dependence and no constant-in-\(P\) term: set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 42. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + Pc2/(Pc3+1)\)
Need rational term vanish: set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 43. \(Pc0(Pc1)^{c2} + Pc3 + c4 e^{c5 t}\)
Need exponential term gone: set \(c4=0\). Then \(c0 c1^{c2} P^{1+c2} + c3 P\). Choose \(c2=-2/3\), \(c0 c1^{c2}=0.1010081\), \(c3=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 44. \(P^{c0}P^{c1}c2 + P^{c0}c3 + c4 e^{c5 t}\)
Need \(c4=0\). Then \(c2 P^{c0+c1} + c3 P^{c0}\): sum of two powers. Choose \(c0=1/3\) and \(c0+c1=1\Rightarrow c1=2/3\). Then expression is \(c2 P + c3 P^{1/3}\). Set \(c2=c3=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 45. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2\log(Pc3+1)\)
Need log term gone: set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 46. \(Pc0(Pc1)^{c2} + Pc3 + c4 t e^{c5 t}\)
Need last term gone: set \(c4=0\). Then same as #43; choose \(c2=-2/3\), etc. **Matches.**

### 47. \(P^{1/3}c0 + P^2 c1 + Pc2 + Pc3\)
Need no \(P^2\) term: set \(c1=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0 + P(c2+c3)\). Choose \(c0=0.1010081\), \(c2+c3=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 48. \(P^{1/3}c0 + P^2 c1 + P^2 c2 + Pc3 + Pc4\)
Set \(c1=0\), \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0 + P(c3+c4)\). Choose coefficients to match. **Matches.**

### 49. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + Pc2/(Pc3+c4) + c5/(Pc3+c4)\)
To avoid extra rational dependence, set \(c2=0\), \(c5=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 50. \(Pc0 + P^{c1}c2 + P^{c3}c4 + c5 + c6 t\)
Need \(c6=0\), \(c5=0\). Then sum of three \(P\)-powers. We can set one extra term to zero, e.g. \(c4=0\), leaving \(Pc0 + c2 P^{c1}\). Choose \(c0=0.1010081\), \(c1=1/3\), \(c2=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 51. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + P^{c2}c3 e^{c4 t}\)
Need remove \(t\)-dependence: either \(c3=0\) (then no \(P^{c2}\) term) or \(c4=0\). If set \(c4=0\), expression is \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c3 P^{c2}\). Set \(c3=0\) to drop extra power and match via \(c0,c1\); or set \(c2=1\) and absorb into linear term (but then would duplicate \(P\)). Easiest: \(c3=0\). Then match. **Matches.**

### 52. \(P^{1/3}c0 + P^3 c1 + P^2 c2 + P^2 c3 + Pc4 + Pc5\)
Set \(c1=0\), \(c2=0\), \(c3=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0 + P(c4+c5)\). Choose to match. **Matches.**

### 53. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + P^{c2}c3\)
Set \(c3=0\) to remove extra power. Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 54. \(Pc0\frac{t}{c1+t} + P^{c2}c3 + P^{c4}c5 + c6\frac{t}{c7+t}\)
Need \(t\)-terms gone: set \(c0=0\), \(c6=0\). Then sum of two powers \(c3 P^{c2}+c5 P^{c4}\). Choose \(c2=1/3\), \(c3=0.1010081\), \(c4=1\), \(c5=0.1010081\). **Matches.**

### 55. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2\exp(c3\sin(c4 t+c5))\)
Last term depends on \(t\) and is also independent of \(P\). Must set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 56. \(P^{1/3}c0 + P^2 c1 e^{c2 t} + Pc3 + Pc4\)
Need no \(P^2\) term: set \(c1=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0 + P(c3+c4)\). Choose to match. **Matches.**

### 57. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2 t (P+c3)^{c4}\)
To remove \(t\)-dependence, set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 58. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2\log(c3 e^{Pc4}+1)\)
Need log term gone: set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 59. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + Pc2(Pc3)^{c4} + Pc5\)
Middle extra term is \(c2 c3^{c4} P^{1+c4}\). To avoid extra power, either set \(c2=0\) (simplest) giving \(P^{1/3}c0 + P(c1+c5)\), or set \(c4=0\) making it linear and absorb into linear coefficient. In either case can match. **Matches.**

### 60. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2\log(c3 e^{Pc4+c5 t}+1)\)
Has \(t\)-dependence unless \(c5=0\) and even then introduces non-polynomial in \(P\). Easiest: set \(c2=0\) to remove the log term entirely. Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 61. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2 e^{Pc3}\)
To match GT, must remove exponential-in-\(P\) term: set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 62. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + c2 e^{Pc3}\log(c4 t+1)\)
Remove extra term by \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**

### 63. \(P^{1/3}c0 + Pc1 + Pc2 e^{Pc3}\)
Need last term gone: set \(c2=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}c0+Pc1\). Set to GT. **Matches.**
